2:58

3:04

3:11

3:48

4:02

4:09

Executive Function
7:20
eliminating as many Superfluous decisions as possible so I'm not
7:26

7:32

7:45

7:51

7:57

8:02

8:08

8:14

8:20

8:27

8:33

8:39
